Burton talks about spiritual preparation.*NewVideo*October 2014 General Conference - Priesthood Session**hPM4cf--w-M**{u'url': u'https://i.ytimg.com/vi/hPM4cf--w-M/default.jpg', u'width': 120, u'height': 90}**General conference is a semiannual gathering of The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints. During general conference weekend, Church members and others gather worldwide in a series of two-hour sessions to receive inspiration and guidance from Church leaders. 

Conference sessions are held the first weekends in April and October. They are held Saturdays and Sundays at 10:00 a.m. and 2:00 p.m. mountain time. The proceeding are broadcast live through a variety of delivery channels, as well as provided in text, audio, and video formats for further study and sharing. Visit gc.lds.org for more details.*NewVideo*Highlight: The Joyful Burden of Discipleship—Ronald A.
